    (function() {
        'use strict';
        var isPremiumHost = location.hostname.indexOf('premium') === 0;
        var isPremiumUser = false, i;
        var cookies = document.cookie.split(/;\s*/);

        for (i = 0; i !== cookies.length; i++) {
            if (cookies[i].indexOf('is_compass_premium=true') === 0) {
                isPremiumUser = true;
                break;
            }
        }

        if (isPremiumUser) {
            if(!isPremiumHost) {
                if (location.hostname.indexOf('www') === 0) {
                    location.href = location.href.replace('www', 'premium');
                }
            }
        }
        else if (isPremiumHost) {
            if (!isPremiumUser) {
                location.href = location.href.replace('premium', 'www');
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

                        <div class="intro-content">
                            <p>
                                Ranked in 2017

">Best Business Schools Rankings Methodology</a>
                                </span>
                            </p>

                            <div class="description-wrapper">
                                <p>A career in business starts with finding the MBA program that fits your needs. With the U.S. News rankings of the top business schools, narrow your search by location, tuition, school size and test scores.</p>
                            </div>
